data-hpc="true">\u003Carticle class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text">\u003Cp align="center" dir="auto"> \u003Ca href="https://github.com/actions/checkout">\u003Cimg alt="GitHub Actions status" src="https://github.com/actions/checkout/workflows/test-local/badge.svg" style="max-width: 100%;">\u003C/a> \u003C/p> \u003Cdiv class="markdown-heading" dir="auto">\u003Ch1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Checkout V2\u003C/h1>\u003Ca id="user-content-checkout-v2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Checkout V2" href="#checkout-v2">\u003Csvg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">\u003Cpath d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z">\u003C/path>\u003C/svg>\u003C/a>\u003C/div> \u003Cp dir="auto">This action checks-out your repository under \u003Ccode>$GITHUB_WORKSPACE\u003C/code>, so your workflow can access it.\u003C/p> \u003Cp dir="auto">Only a single commit is fetched by default, for the ref/SHA that triggered the workflow. Set \u003Ccode>fetch-depth: 0\u003C/code> to fetch all history for all branches and tags. Refer \u003Ca href="https://help.github.com/en/articles/events-that-trigger-workflows">here\u003C/a> to learn which commit \u003Ccode>$GITHUB_SHA\u003C/code> points to for different events.\u003C/p> \u003Cp dir="auto">The auth token is persisted in the local git config. This enables your scripts to run authenticated git commands. The token is removed during post-job cleanup. Set \u003Ccode>persist-credentials: false\u003C/code> to opt-out.\u003C/p> \u003Cp dir="auto">When Git 2.18 or higher is not in your PATH, falls back to the REST API to download the files.\u003C/p> \u003Cdiv class="markdown-heading" dir="auto">\u003Ch1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">What's new\u003C/h1>\u003Ca id="user-content-whats-new" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z">\u003C/path>\u003C/svg>\u003C/a>\u003C/div> \u003Cul dir="auto"> \u003Cli>Improved performance \u003Cul dir="auto"> \u003Cli>Fetches only a single commit by default\u003C/li> \u003C/ul> \u003C/li> \u003Cli>Script authenticated git commands \u003Cul dir="auto"> \u003Cli>Auth token persisted in the local git config\u003C/li> \u003C/ul> \u003C/li> \u003Cli>Supports SSH\u003C/li> \u003Cli>Creates a local branch \u003Cul dir="auto"> \u003Cli>No longer detached HEAD when checking out a branch\u003C/li> \u003C/ul> \u003C/li> \u003Cli>Improved layout \u003Cul dir="auto"> \u003Cli>The input \u003Ccode>path\u003C/code> is always relative to $GITHUB_WORKSPACE\u003C/li> \u003Cli>Aligns better with container actions, where $GITHUB_WORKSPACE gets mapped in\u003C/li> \u003C/ul> \u003C/li> \u003Cli>Fallback to REST API download \u003Cul dir="auto"> \u003Cli>When Git 2.18 or higher is not in the PATH, the REST API will be used to download the files\u003C/li> \u003Cli>When using a job container, the container's PATH is used\u003C/li> \u003C/ul> \u003C/li> \u003C/ul> \u003Cp dir="auto">Refer \u003Ca href="https://github.com/actions/checkout/blob/v1/README.md">here\u003C/a> for previous versions.\u003C/p> \u003Cdiv class="markdown-heading" dir="auto">\u003Ch1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Usage\u003C/h1>\u003Ca id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Usage" href="#usage">\u003Csvg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">\u003Cpath d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z">\u003C/path>\u003C/svg>\u003C/a>\u003C/div> \u003Cdiv class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto">\u003Cpre>- \u003Cspan class="pl-ent">uses\u003C/span>: \u003Cspan class="pl-s">actions/checkout@v2\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-ent">with\u003C/span>: \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> Repository name with owner. For example, actions/checkout\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> Default: ${{ github.repository }}\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-ent">repository\u003C/span>: \u003Cspan class="pl-s">\u003Cspan class="pl-pds">'\u003C/span>\u003Cspan class="pl-pds">'\u003C/span>\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> The branch, tag or SHA to checkout. When checking out the repository that\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> triggered a workflow, this defaults to the reference or SHA for that event.\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> Otherwise, uses the default branch.\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-ent">ref\u003C/span>: \u003Cspan class="pl-s">\u003Cspan class="pl-pds">'\u003C/span>\u003Cspan class="pl-pds">'\u003C/span>\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> Personal access token (PAT) used to fetch the repository. The PAT is configured\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> with the local git config, which enables your scripts to run authenticated git\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> commands. The post-job step removes the PAT.\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span>\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> We recommend using a service account with the least permissions necessary. Also\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> when generating a new PAT, select the least scopes necessary.\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span>\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> [Learn more about creating and using encrypted secrets](https://help.github.com/en/actions/automating-your-workflow-with-github-actions/creating-and-using-encrypted-secrets)\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span>\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> Default: ${{ github.token }}\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-ent">token\u003C/span>: \u003Cspan class="pl-s">\u003Cspan class="pl-pds">'\u003C/span>\u003Cspan class="pl-pds">'\u003C/span>\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> SSH key used to fetch the repository. The SSH key is configured with the local\u003C/span> \u003Cspan class="pl-c">\u003Cspan class="pl-c">#\u003C/span> git config, which enables your scripts to run authenticated git commands.
